$$= 23.788\epsilon \cdot (-0.05042T + 0.05042 \cdot 330.2 + 1) + 5.2295\epsilon^{0.9585}(T - 330.2)$$
$$= 23.788\epsilon(-0.05042T + 17.645) + 5.2295\epsilon^{0.9585}T - 5.2295 \cdot 330.2 \cdot \epsilon^{0.9585}$$

3. $T \cdot \epsilon^{0.9585}$ (T times fractional power of epsilon)
